\chapter*{Preface}\label{preface}
\addcontentsline{toc}{chapter}{Preface}

\markboth{Preface}{Preface}

This scientific project is actively being developed for investigating
OTIS Data.\footnote{Service Management and Oversight Branch's detailed
  data collection of restrictive confinement placements (A01RCDD) in
  Ontario's Adult Correctional System is maintained by the Business
  Intelligence and Insights Branch of the Ministry of the Solicitor
  General. For the partial MECA Bundle, see
  \url{https://vanshsinghruhela-statistical-report-on-restrictive-confinement.share.connect.posit.cloud}.}

\bookmarksetup{startatroot}

\chapter{Introduction}\label{introduction}

\subsection{A01-RC Detailed Dataset}\label{a01-rc-detailed-dataset}

The following analysis utilizes the Restrictive Confinement Detailed
Dataset (A01RCDD) maintained by the Service Management and Oversight
Branch of Ontario's Ministry of the Solicitor General
\autocite{Ontario_SOLGEN_DataOnInmatesOntario_2025,Ontario_SOLGEN_RC_DetailedDataset_2025}.
This administrative data collection tracks all restrictive confinement
placements in Ontario's adult correctional system, including segregation
practices and associated demographic information.

The dataset is publicly accessible through the Ontario Open Data portal
\autocite{Ontario_SOLGEN_DataOnInmatesOntario_2025} and can be queried
programmatically via the CKAN Data API \autocite{Ontario_CKAN_API_2025}.
Data collection follows protocols established under the \emph{Jahn v.
Ontario} settlement agreement \autocite{Ontario_JahnSettlement_2025} and
relevant provincial legislation
\autocite{Ontario_MCSCS_Act,Ontario_Correctional_Services_Act}.

\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(DoubleML)}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(mlr3)}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(mlr3learners)}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(data.table)}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(dplyr)}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(parallel)}
\NormalTok{lgr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{get\_logger}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"mlr3"}\NormalTok{)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\FunctionTok{set\_threshold}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"warn"}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\# "regr.lm" instead of "regr.ranger" utilized (disclaimer)}
\CommentTok{\# "classif.log\_reg", predict\_type = "prob" instead of classif.ranger}
\CommentTok{\# cores \textless{}{-} max(1L, parallel::detectCores() {-} 1L)}
\CommentTok{\# yn\_cols \textless{}{-} c("mental\_health\_alert", "suicide\_risk\_alert", "suicide\_watch\_alert")}
\CommentTok{\# dfn \textless{}{-} dfn \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   mutate(across(}
\CommentTok{\#     all\_of(yn\_cols),}
\CommentTok{\#     \textasciitilde{} factor(dplyr::if\_else(.x == "Yes", 1L, 0L), levels = c(0, 1))}
\CommentTok{\#   ))}
\CommentTok{\# dt \textless{}{-} as.data.table(dfn)}
\CommentTok{\# dt[, number\_of\_placements := as.integer(number\_of\_placements)]}
\CommentTok{\# dt \textless{}{-} dt[!is.na(number\_of\_placements) \& number\_of\_placements \textgreater{} 0L]}
\CommentTok{\# N\_expanded \textless{}{-} sum(dt$number\_of\_placements)}
\CommentTok{\# message("Expanded N = ", format(N\_expanded, big.mark = ","))}
\CommentTok{\# dt \textless{}{-} dt[rep.int(seq\_len(.N), number\_of\_placements)]}
\CommentTok{\# dt[, Y := as.integer(suicide\_risk\_alert) {-} 1L]}
\CommentTok{\# dt[, D := as.integer(mental\_health\_alert) {-} 1L]}
\CommentTok{\# stopifnot(identical(sort(unique(dt$D)), c(0L, 1L)))}
\CommentTok{\# dt[, cluster\_id := as.factor(unique\_individual\_id)]}
\CommentTok{\# ml\_g \textless{}{-} lrn("regr.lm")}
\CommentTok{\# ml\_m \textless{}{-} lrn("classif.log\_reg", predict\_type = "prob")}
\CommentTok{\# fit\_irm\_ate\_atte \textless{}{-} function(dsub, x\_cols, tag) \{}
\CommentTok{\#   dml\_data \textless{}{-} DoubleMLClusterData$new(}
\CommentTok{\#     data = dsub,}
\CommentTok{\#     y\_col = "Y",}
\CommentTok{\#     d\_cols = "D",}
\CommentTok{\#     x\_cols = x\_cols,}
\CommentTok{\#     cluster\_cols = "cluster\_id"}
\CommentTok{\#   )}
\CommentTok{\#   set.seed(1111111111)}
\CommentTok{\#   obj\_ate \textless{}{-} DoubleMLIRM$new(}
\CommentTok{\#     dml\_data,}
\CommentTok{\#     ml\_g = ml\_g,}
\CommentTok{\#     ml\_m = ml\_m,}
\CommentTok{\#     n\_folds = 3,}
\CommentTok{\#     n\_rep = 1,}
\CommentTok{\#     score = "ATE"}
\CommentTok{\#   )}
\CommentTok{\#   obj\_ate$fit()}
\CommentTok{\#   set.seed(1111111111)}
\CommentTok{\#   obj\_atte \textless{}{-} DoubleMLIRM$new(}
\CommentTok{\#     dml\_data,}
\CommentTok{\#     ml\_g = ml\_g,}
\CommentTok{\#     ml\_m = ml\_m,}
\CommentTok{\#     n\_folds = 3,}
\CommentTok{\#     n\_rep = 1,}
\CommentTok{\#     score = "ATTE"}
\CommentTok{\#   )}
\CommentTok{\#   obj\_atte$fit()}
\CommentTok{\#   mk \textless{}{-} function(obj, estimand) \{}
\CommentTok{\#     ci \textless{}{-} obj$confint(level = 0.95)}
\CommentTok{\#     data.table(}
\CommentTok{\#       group = tag,}
\CommentTok{\#       estimand = estimand,}
\CommentTok{\#       effect = as.numeric(obj$coef),}
\CommentTok{\#       se = as.numeric(obj$se),}
\CommentTok{\#       t\_value = as.numeric(obj$t\_stat),}
\CommentTok{\#       p\_value = as.numeric(obj$pval),}
\CommentTok{\#       ci\_low = as.numeric(ci[1, 1]),}
\CommentTok{\#       ci\_high = as.numeric(ci[1, 2])}
\CommentTok{\#     )}
\CommentTok{\#   \}}
\CommentTok{\#   rbind(mk(obj\_ate, "ATE"), mk(obj\_atte, "ATTE"))}
\CommentTok{\# \}}
\CommentTok{\# x\_cols\_pool \textless{}{-} c(}
\CommentTok{\#   "gender",}
\CommentTok{\#   "age\_category",}
\CommentTok{\#   "region\_at\_time\_of\_placement",}
\CommentTok{\#   "region\_most\_recent\_placement",}
\CommentTok{\#   "end\_fiscal\_year"}
\CommentTok{\# )}
\CommentTok{\# dt[, (x\_cols\_pool) := lapply(.SD, as.factor), .SDcols = x\_cols\_pool]}
\CommentTok{\# keep\_pool \textless{}{-} complete.cases(dt[,}
\CommentTok{\#   c("Y", "D", "cluster\_id", x\_cols\_pool),}
\CommentTok{\#   with = FALSE}
\CommentTok{\# ])}
\CommentTok{\# dsub\_pool \textless{}{-} dt[keep\_pool, c("Y", "D", "cluster\_id", x\_cols\_pool), with = FALSE]}
\CommentTok{\# res\_pool \textless{}{-} fit\_irm\_ate\_atte(dsub\_pool, x\_cols\_pool, tag = "Pooled 2023{-}25")}
\CommentTok{\# years \textless{}{-} sort(unique(dt$end\_fiscal\_year))}
\CommentTok{\# x\_cols\_year \textless{}{-} c(}
\CommentTok{\#   "gender",}
\CommentTok{\#   "age\_category",}
\CommentTok{\#   "region\_at\_time\_of\_placement",}
\CommentTok{\#   "region\_most\_recent\_placement"}
\CommentTok{\# )}
\CommentTok{\# res\_by\_year \textless{}{-} rbindlist(lapply(years, function(yy) \{}
\CommentTok{\#   sub \textless{}{-} dt[end\_fiscal\_year == yy]}
\CommentTok{\#   sub[, (x\_cols\_year) := lapply(.SD, as.factor), .SDcols = x\_cols\_year]}
\CommentTok{\#   keep\_y \textless{}{-} complete.cases(sub[,}
\CommentTok{\#     c("Y", "D", "cluster\_id", x\_cols\_year),}
\CommentTok{\#     with = FALSE}
\CommentTok{\#   ])}
\CommentTok{\#   dsub\_y \textless{}{-} sub[keep\_y, c("Y", "D", "cluster\_id", x\_cols\_year), with = FALSE]}
\CommentTok{\#   fit\_irm\_ate\_atte(dsub\_y, x\_cols\_year, tag = as.character(yy))}
\CommentTok{\# \}))}

\CommentTok{\# person{-}year: alert{-}state intensity via 2\^{}3 = 8 possible outcomes (a1{-}a8) where two (a3 and a6) were not observed empirically}

    \AttributeTok{a1 =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{((combo }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"a1"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ np, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}

\CommentTok{\# 6. VOLATILITY (v\_moves): placement transfers/shifts within the person{-}year sequence for vm}

\NormalTok{  .(}
    \AttributeTok{vm =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{((regA }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ regB) }\SpecialCharTok{|}\NormalTok{ (regA }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \FunctionTok{shift}\NormalTok{(regA) }\SpecialCharTok{\&} \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{shift}\NormalTok{(regA))))}
\NormalTok{  ),}

\NormalTok{]}

  \FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{16254911}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{  extract }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(obj, est) \{}
\NormalTok{    ci }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ obj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\FunctionTok{confint}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{level =} \FloatTok{0.95}\NormalTok{)}
    \FunctionTok{data.table}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{method =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Clustered by "}\NormalTok{, cluster\_var),}
      \AttributeTok{group =}\NormalTok{ tag,}
      \AttributeTok{estimand =}\NormalTok{ est,}
      \AttributeTok{effect =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(obj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{coef),}
      \AttributeTok{se =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(obj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{se),}
      \AttributeTok{p\_value =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(obj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pval),}
      \AttributeTok{ci\_low =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(ci[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]),}
      \AttributeTok{ci\_high =} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(ci[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{extract}\NormalTok{(obj\_ate, }\StringTok{"ATE"}\NormalTok{), }\FunctionTok{extract}\NormalTok{(obj\_atte, }\StringTok{"ATTE"}\NormalTok{)))}
\NormalTok{\}}
